<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дунуть.html>ду́нуть</a> (12632)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>дуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дунуть.html>ду́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dúnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to blow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rush, to hasten, to dash
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дунуть.html>ду́нул</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оттуда.html>отту́да</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on kak <b>dúnul</b> ottúda!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he ran away like a bat out of hell!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***дурак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дурак</a> (890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дура́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">durák</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дурака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дураки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дурако́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дура.html>ду́ра</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fool, simpleton, idiot <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">stupid person with poor judgment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>a simple card game in which the last player holding cards in their hand is the loser</li></ol>

***дуреющий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дуреющий.html>дуре́ющий</a> (29034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуреющий.html>дуре́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">duréjuščij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурить.html>дури́ть</a> (17472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duriti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурить.html>дури́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">durítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to frolic, to play pranks, to be naughty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to behave like a fool
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>дури</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne duri!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't be foolish!; don't make a fool of yourself!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be obstinate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fool
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дурить.html>дури́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голову</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>durítʹ</b> golovu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to confuse smb; mix smb up</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурман.html>дурма́н</a> (20087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A Russian formation based on <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>дурно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">durnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красивый.html>краси́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krasívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нехороший.html>нехоро́ший</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nexoróšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дура.html>ду́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ныть.html>но́й</a></b>

***дурость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурость.html>ду́рость</a> (17945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дура.html>ду́р</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:ныть.html>но́й</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dur(nój)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурость.html>ду́рость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dúrostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурость.html>ду́рости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурость.html>ду́рости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурость.html>ду́ростей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stupidity, folly</li></ol>

***дуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>дуть</a> (4081)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dǫti</i> from Early <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dъm-ti</i>, from the root of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dymъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>дым</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dym</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">damp</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>дуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подуть.html>поду́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дунуть.html>ду́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Véter <b>dújet</b> nam v licó.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The wind is blowing into our faces.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be drafty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>Здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́ет</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zdesʹ <b>dújet</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There is a draft here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go quickly, to scamper
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсюда.html>отсю́да</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A nu <b>duj</b> otsjúda!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Off with you quickly!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дуться.html>ду́ться</a> (19755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуться.html>ду́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуться.html>наду́ться</a></b>)
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duxъ</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>дух</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>dux</a></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́хов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spirit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́хе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne v dúxe</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in a bad temper</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mind</li>

<li>rebel (especially in Afghanistan; from <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>душман</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dušman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> new recruit, rookie who is sometimes abused by the longer serving soldiers</li></ol>

<ol><li>shower <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">device for bathing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***душа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа</a> (236)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">доуша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">duša</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soul</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duša</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dušá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>души́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>soul
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>души́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot <b>duší</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from the heart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нараспашку.html>нараспа́шку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>duša</b> naraspášku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">frank-hearted, heart on one's sleeve</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глубина.html>глубине́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>души́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v glubiné <b>duší</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">deep in one's heart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bratʹ zá <b>dušu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">touch the heart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>duša</b> v <b>dúšu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in perfect harmony/concord</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душа́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dušá</b> ne na méste</i> ― <span class="e-translation">anxious, worried</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душе́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne po <b>dušé</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">displeases</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душе́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>dušé</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pleasant</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кривить.html>криви́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душо́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krivítʹ <b>dušój</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to equivocate, prevaricate, bend the truth</span></div></dd>
